## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where dv/dt depends on position x, velocity v, and possibly time t through restoring forces, damping, nonlinear terms, and potential external driving.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (Duffing + damping)
- Driven damped oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * cos(c3 * t) (with periodic driving)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (full Duffing)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (c2 + c3 * x**2) (nonlinear damping)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force)
- Quintic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinearity)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * x (position-dependent damping)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Mixed nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v * x**2 + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (general nonlinear driven)
- Mathieu-type: dv_dt = (c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x (parametric excitation)
- Helmholtz oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * v (quadratic nonlinearity with damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x┬│, xтБ╡) тЖТ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power position terms (x┬▓) тЖТ asymmetric potential indicating broken spatial symmetry
- Velocity-position product terms (v┬╖x┬▓, v┬╖x) тЖТ amplitude-dependent or position-dependent damping (Van der Pol type)
- Sinusoidal time dependence cos(c┬╖t) тЖТ external periodic driving force; look for resonance phenomena
- Parametric modulation (x┬╖cos(c┬╖t)) тЖТ parametric excitation where system parameters vary periodically
- Cubic velocity terms (v┬│) тЖТ Rayleigh-type nonlinear dissipation modeling air resistance or self-excitation
- Sign of cubic position coefficient opposite to linear тЖТ softening (same sign) vs hardening (opposite sign) spring behavior
- Absence of explicit time dependence тЖТ autonomous system; energy conservation or limit cycle behavior
- sin(c┬╖x) as restoring force тЖТ large-amplitude pendulum dynamics where small-angle approximation fails
- Negative linear damping with positive nonlinear damping (c1┬╖v + c2┬╖v┬╖x┬▓) тЖТ self-sustained oscillations with amplitude limiting
